The_DT Superintendent_NNP 's_POS report_NN is_VBZ self-contained_JJ ,_, full_JJ and_CC complete_JJ ,_, but_CC the_DT following_JJ general_JJ remarks_NNS are_VBP made_VBN thereon_JJ :2_JJ suffering_VBG from_IN Tubercle_NNP of_IN the_DT lung_NN showed_VBD an_DT increase_NN of_IN 8_CD in_IN 1914_CD ,_, the_DT figures_NNS being_VBG 13_CD in_IN 1914_CD ,_, 5_CD in_IN 1913_CD and_CC 9_CD in_IN 1912_CD ._.

The_DT death-rates_NNS in_IN 1914_CD in_IN the_DT asylums_NNS in_IN the_DT other_JJ Provinces_NNPS were:3_JJ arrangements_NNS for_IN drinking_NN water_NN ,_, cooking_NN ,_, bathing_NN and_CC conservancy_NN are_VBP all_DT very_RB satisfactory_JJ ._.

The_DT establishment_NN of_IN the_DT asylum_NN also_RB worked_VBD as_RB well_RB as_IN could_MD be_VB expected_VBN under_IN the_DT circumstances_NNS ._.
10_CD ._.
The_DT new_JJ Indian_JJ Lunacy_NNP Act_NNP was_VBD introduced_VBN during_IN the_DT year_NN 1912_CD ,_, and_CC in_IN 1913_CD all_PDT the_DT districts_NNS of_IN the_DT Province_NNP of_IN Bihar_NNP and_CC Orissa_NNP ,_, including_VBG the_DT district_NN of_IN Angul_NNP ,_, were_VBD declared_VBN to_TO be_VB areas_NNS in_IN which_WDT reception_NN orders_NNS may_MD be_VB made_VBN under_IN the_DT provisions_NNS of_IN the_DT Act_NNP ._.
